#ELECTION DECISION
GRE_1936_election_category = { 
	GRE_the_election_of_1936  = { # Election crisis

		icon = eng_support_imperialist_coup
        on_map_mode = map_and_decisions_view

        highlight_states = {
 			highlight_state_targets = { state = 47 } 
 			#highlight_color_before_active = 3
			highlight_color_while_active = 1
		}

		allowed = { tag=GRE }

		available = {
			date > 1936.01.26
		}

		days_mission_timeout = 26

		fire_only_once = yes

		activation = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = GRE_1936_election }
		}

		visible = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = GRE_1936_election }
		}

		cancel_if_not_visible = no

		is_good = no

		complete_effect = {
			#hidden_effect = { 
                country_event = { id = hellenic_news.1 days = 7 }
				set_country_flag = GRE_1936_election
                complete_national_focus = GRE_election_1936
			#}
		}
	}

	GRE_the_election_of_1936_cont  = { # Election crisis

		icon = eng_support_imperialist_coup
        on_map_mode = map_and_decisions_view

        highlight_states = {
 			highlight_state_targets = { state = 47 } 
 			#highlight_color_before_active = 3
			highlight_color_while_active = 1
		}

		allowed = { tag=GRE }

		available = {
			date > 1936.03.5
		}

		days_mission_timeout = 37

		fire_only_once = yes

		activation = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = GRE_1936_election_cont }
            has_country_flag = GRE_1936_election
		}

		visible = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = GRE_1936_election_cont }
		}

		cancel_if_not_visible = no

		is_good = no

		complete_effect = {
			hidden_effect = {
                country_event = { id = hellenic_news.2 days = 7 }
				set_country_flag = GRE_1936_election_cont
                complete_national_focus = GRE_georges_dictat
                set_country_flag = GRE_faction_gui_flag
			}
		}
	}

	GRE_demertzis_death  = { # Election crisis

		icon = eng_support_imperialist_coup
        on_map_mode = map_only
        highlight_states = { highlight_states_trigger = { state = -1 } }

		allowed = { tag=GRE }

		available = {
			has_completed_focus = GRE_escalating_strikes
		}

		days_mission_timeout = 102

		fire_only_once = yes

		activation = {
		}

		visible = {
			is_debug = yes has_country_flag=debug_decs
		}

		cancel_if_not_visible = no

		is_good = no

		complete_effect = {
			hidden_effect = { 
			}
		}

		timeout_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_1936_election_tt
			hidden_effect = { 
                country_event = { id = hellenic_news.3 days = 1 }
			}
		}
	}

	GRE_metaxas_vote_of_confidence_hidden  = { # Election crisis

		icon = eng_support_imperialist_coup
        on_map_mode = map_only
        highlight_states = { highlight_states_trigger = { state = -1 } }

		allowed = { tag=GRE }

		available = {
			has_completed_focus = GRE_escalating_strikes
		}

		days_mission_timeout = 114

		fire_only_once = yes

		activation = {
		}

		visible = {
			is_debug = yes has_country_flag=debug_decs
		}

		cancel_if_not_visible = no

		is_good = no

		complete_effect = {
		}

		timeout_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_1936_election_tt

			}

	GRE_hidden_strikes_misson  = { # Election crisis

#GREECE INVESTMENT DECISIONS
GRE_investment_decisions_category = {

    GRE_expand_collapse_foreign_manufacturer_buffs = {
        icon = decision_generic_decision
    
        allowed = { tag=GRE }
        
        fire_only_once = no
        days_remove = 0
        days_re_enable = 0
        priority = 12
        
        visible = {
            has_completed_focus = GRE_open_up_the_country
            NOT = { has_global_flag = GRE_crete_still_holding }
            NOT = { has_global_flag = GRE_government_in_exile }
        }
        
        complete_effect = {
            hidden_effect = {
                if = {
                    limit = {
                        NOT = { has_country_flag = toggle_fm }
                    }
                    set_country_flag = toggle_fm
                }
                else = {
                    clr_country_flag = toggle_fm 
                }
            }
        }
    }

    GRE_foreign_manufacturer_light_armor_investments = {
        on_map_mode = map_and_decisions_view
        highlight_states = { highlight_states_trigger = { state = FROM.capital } }
        
        icon = generic_tank
		allowed = { tag = GRE }
        priority = 12
        days_re_enable = 550

		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
                OR = {
                    original_tag = GER 
                    original_tag = FRA 
                    original_tag = ENG 
                    original_tag = SOV 
                    original_tag = ITA 
                    original_tag = JAP
                    original_tag = USA 
                }
			}
		}

		available = {
			date < 1942.1.1
            FROM = { exists = yes }
			NOT = {
				has_war_with = FROM
                custom_trigger_tooltip = {
                    tooltip = GRE_favor_abysmal_from_tt
                    check_variable = { var = FROM.favor@GRE value = 0 compare = less_than }
                }
			}
            has_completed_appropriate_fm_focuses = yes
		}
        
		visible = {
            NOT = { has_country_flag = toggle_fm }
			has_completed_focus = GRE_open_up_the_country
            NOT = { has_global_flag = GRE_crete_still_holding }
            NOT = { has_global_flag = GRE_government_in_exile }
            has_appropriate_armor_fm_selected = yes
		}
        
        days_remove = 14
        cost = 25

		remove_effect = {
            #####################[Domestic Competition Limits]####################
            if = {
                limit = { has_idea = GRE_domestic_competition_0_hidden }
                set_temp_variable = { bonus_from_domcom_level = 0.60 }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = { has_idea = GRE_domestic_competition_1_hidden }
                set_temp_variable = { bonus_from_domcom_level = 0.40 }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = { has_idea = GRE_domestic_competition_2_hidden }
                set_temp_variable = { bonus_from_domcom_level = 0.10 }
            }
            else = {
                set_temp_variable = { bonus_from_domcom_level = 0.00 }
            }
            ########################[FROM Has Tech Bonus]########################
            if = {
                limit = { 
                    FROM = {
                        meta_trigger = {
                            text = { has_tech = [LIGHT_TANK_TECH] }
                            LIGHT_TANK_TECH = "[GRE.GetNextLightTank]"
                        }
                    }
                }
                set_temp_variable = { bonus_from_researched_tech = 0.4 }
            }
            else = {
                set_temp_variable = { bonus_from_researched_tech = 0.1 }
            }
            ##########################[Country Bonuses]##########################
            if = { 
                limit = { FROM = { original_tag = GER } }
                set_temp_variable = { bonus_from_country = 0.1 }
            }
            else_if = { 
                limit = { FROM = { original_tag = SOV } }
                set_temp_variable = { bonus_from_country = 0.1 }
            }
            else_if = { 
                limit = { FROM = { original_tag = FRA } }
                set_temp_variable = { bonus_from_country = 0.12 }
            }
            else_if = { 
                limit = { FROM = { original_tag = ENG } }
                set_temp_variable = { bonus_from_country = 0.1 }
            }
            else_if = { 
                limit = { FROM = { original_tag = USA } }
                set_temp_variable = { bonus_from_country = 0.12 }
            }
            else_if = { 
                limit = { FROM = { original_tag = ITA } }
                set_temp_variable = { bonus_from_country = 0.06 }
            }
            else_if = { 
                limit = { FROM = { original_tag = JAP } }
                set_temp_variable = { bonus_from_country = 0.08 }
            }
            add_bonuses_to_sum = yes
            meta_effect = {
                text = { add_tech_bonus = { name=GRE_FM_light_tank_bonus bonus=[BONUS_SUM] uses=1 technology=[LIGHT_TANK_TECH] } }
                BONUS_SUM = "[?sum|.3]"
                LIGHT_TANK_TECH = "[GRE.GetNextLightTank]"
            }
        }
    }

    GRE_foreign_manufacturer_medium_armor_investments = {
        on_map_mode = map_and_decisions_view
        highlight_states = { highlight_states_trigger = { state = FROM.capital } }

                set_temp_variable = { bonus_from_researched_tech = 0.4 }

            if = {

            }
            else_if = { 
                limit = { FROM = { original_tag = SOV } }
                set_temp_variable = { bonus_from_country = 0.16 }
            }
            else_if = { 
                limit = { FROM = { original_tag = FRA } }
                set_temp_variable = { bonus_from_country = 0.05 }
            }
            else_if = { 
                limit = { FROM = { original_tag = ENG } }
                set_temp_variable = { bonus_from_country = 0.07 }
            }
            else_if = { 
                limit = { FROM = { original_tag = USA } }
                set_temp_variable = { bonus_from_country = 0.08 }
            }
            else_if = { 
                limit = { FROM = { original_tag = ITA } }
                set_temp_variable = { bonus_from_country = 0.02 }
            }
            else_if = { 
                limit = { FROM = { original_tag = JAP } }
                set_temp_variable = { bonus_from_country = 0.01 }
            }
            add_bonuses_to_sum = yes
            meta_effect = {
                text = { add_tech_bonus = { name=GRE_FM_medium_tank_bonus bonus=[BONUS_SUM] uses=1 technology=[MEDIUM_TANK_TECH] } }
                BONUS_SUM = "[?sum|.3]"

    GRE_foreign_manufacturer_naval_screen_investments = {
        icon = generic_naval
        on_map_mode = map_and_decisions_view
        highlight_states = { highlight_states_trigger = { state = FROM.capital } }

		allowed = { tag = GRE }
        priority = 12
        days_re_enable = 550
		target_trigger = { FROM = { OR = { original_tag = ENG original_tag = JAP original_tag = USA original_tag = GER } } }

		available = {
			date < 1942.1.1
            FROM = { exists = yes }
			NOT = {
				has_war_with = FROM
                custom_trigger_tooltip = {
                    tooltip = GRE_favor_abysmal_from_tt
                    check_variable = { var = FROM.favor@GRE value = 0 compare = less_than }
                }
			}
            has_completed_appropriate_fm_focuses = yes
		}
        
		visible = {
            NOT = { has_country_flag = toggle_fm }
			has_completed_focus = GRE_open_up_the_country
            NOT = { has_global_flag = GRE_crete_still_holding }
            NOT = { has_global_flag = GRE_government_in_exile }
            has_appropriate_naval_fm_selected = yes
		}
        
        days_remove = 14
        cost = 250

		remove_effect = {
            #[Destroyer Hull]#
            if = {
                limit = {
                    FROM = {
                        meta_trigger = {
                            text = { has_tech = [DESTR] }
                            DESTR = "[GRE.GetNextDestroyer]"
                        }
                    }
                }
                set_temp_variable = { fm_destroyer_bonus = 0.75 }
            }
            else = {
                set_temp_variable = { fm_destroyer_bonus = 0.25 }
            }
            #[Cruiser Hull]#
            if = {
                limit = {
                    FROM = {
                        meta_trigger = {
                            text = { has_tech = [CRU] }
                            CRU = "[GRE.GetNextCruiser]"
                        }
                    }
                }
                set_temp_variable = { fm_cruiser_bonus = 0.75 }
            }
            else = {
                set_temp_variable = { fm_cruiser_bonus = 0.25 }
            }
            #[Destroyer SubTechs]#
            if = {
                limit = {
                    FROM = {
                        meta_trigger = {
                            text = { has_tech = [ITEM] }
                            ITEM = "[GRE.GetNextDestrDepth]"
                        }
                    }
                }
                set_temp_variable = { fm_destroyer_sonar_bonus = 0.75 }
            }
            else = {
                set_temp_variable = { fm_destroyer_sonar_bonus = 0.25 }
            }
            if = {
                limit = { 
                    FROM = {
                        meta_trigger = {
                            text = { has_tech = [ITEM] }
                            ITEM = "[GRE.GetNextDestrDepth]"
                        }
                    }
                }
                set_temp_variable = { fm_destroyer_depth_bonus = 0.75 }
            }
            else = {
                set_temp_variable = { fm_destroyer_depth_bonus = 0.25 }
            }
            #[Cruiser SubTechs]#
            if = {
                limit = {
                    FROM = {
                        meta_trigger = {
                            text = { has_tech = [ITEM] }
                            ITEM = "[GRE.GetNextCruCatapult]"
                        }
                    }
                }
                set_temp_variable = { fm_cruiser_catap_bonus = 0.75 }
            }
            else = {
                set_temp_variable = { fm_cruiser_catap_bonus = 0.25 }
            }
            if = {
                limit = { 
                    FROM = {
                        meta_trigger = {
                            text = { has_tech = [ITEM] }
                            ITEM = "[GRE.GetNextCruArmor]"
                        }
                    }
                }
                set_temp_variable = { fm_cruiser_armor_bonus = 0.75 }
            }
            else = {
                set_temp_variable = { fm_cruiser_armor_bonus = 0.25 }
            }
            ###[Final Effects]###
            meta_effect = {
                text = {
                    if = { limit = { NOT = { has_tech = [ITEM] } } 
                        add_tech_bonus = { name=GRE_FM_screen_bonus bonus=[BONS] uses=1 technology=[ITEM] }
                    }
                }
                BONS = "[?fm_destroyer_bonus|.3]"
                ITEM = "[GRE.GetNextDestroyer]"
            }
            meta_effect = {
                text = {
                    if = { limit = { NOT = { has_tech = [ITEM] } } 
                        add_tech_bonus = { name=GRE_FM_screen_bonus bonus=[BONS] uses=1 technology=[ITEM] }
                    }
                }
                BONS = "[?fm_destroyer_depth_bonus|.3]"
                ITEM = "[GRE.GetNextDestrDepth]"
            }
            meta_effect = {
                text = {
                    if = { limit = { NOT = { has_tech = [ITEM] } } 
                        add_tech_bonus = { name=GRE_FM_screen_bonus bonus=[BONS] uses=1 technology=[ITEM] }
                    }
                }
                BONS = "[?fm_destroyer_sonar_bonus|.3]"
                ITEM = "[GRE.GetNextDestrSonar]"
            }
            meta_effect = {
                text = {
                    if = { limit = { NOT = { has_tech = [ITEM] } } 
                        add_tech_bonus = { name=GRE_FM_screen_bonus bonus=[BONS] uses=1 technology=[ITEM] }
                    }
                }

                ITEM = "[GRE.GetNextCruiser]"
            }
            meta_effect = {

                    if = { limit = { NOT = { has_tech = [ITEM] } }

            else_if = {

                set_temp_variable = { bonus_from_domcom_level = 0.40 }

                            text = { has_tech = [ITEM] }

                        }

                }
                set_temp_variable = { bonus_from_researched_tech = 0.4 }
            }

                set_temp_variable = { bonus_from_country = 0.06 }
            }
            else_if = { 
                limit = { FROM = { original_tag = JAP } }
                set_temp_variable = { bonus_from_country = 0.06 }
            }
            add_bonuses_to_sum = yes
            meta_effect = {

    GRE_foreign_manufacturer_cas_investments = {
        on_map_mode = map_and_decisions_view
        highlight_states = { highlight_states_trigger = { state = FROM.capital } }
        
        icon = generic_air
		allowed = { tag = GRE }
        priority = 12
        days_re_enable = 550

		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
                OR = {
                    original_tag = GER 
                    original_tag = FRA 
                    original_tag = ENG 
                    original_tag = SOV 
                    original_tag = JAP
                    original_tag = USA 
                }
			}
		}

		available = {
			date < 1942.1.1
            FROM = { exists = yes }
			NOT = {
				has_war_with = FROM
                custom_trigger_tooltip = {
                    tooltip = GRE_favor_abysmal_from_tt
                    check_variable = { var = FROM.favor@GRE value = 0 compare = less_than }
                }
			}
            has_completed_appropriate_fm_focuses = yes
		}
        
		visible = {
            NOT = { has_country_flag = toggle_fm }
			has_completed_focus = GRE_open_up_the_country
            NOT = { has_global_flag = GRE_crete_still_holding }
            NOT = { has_global_flag = GRE_government_in_exile }
            has_appropriate_aircraft_fm_selected = yes
		}
        
        days_remove = 14
        cost = 25

		remove_effect = {
            #####################[Domestic Competition Limits]####################
            if = {

                set_temp_variable = { bonus_from_domcom_level = 0.60 }

        days_re_enable = 550

		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
                OR = {
                    original_tag = ITA
                    original_tag = JAP
                }
			}
		}

		available = {
			date < 1942.1.1
            FROM = { exists = yes }
			NOT = {
				has_war_with = FROM
                custom_trigger_tooltip = {
                    tooltip = GRE_favor_abysmal_from_tt
                    check_variable = { var = FROM.favor@GRE value = 0 compare = less_than }
                }
			}
            has_completed_appropriate_fm_focuses = yes
		}
        
		visible = {
            NOT = { has_country_flag = toggle_fm }
			has_completed_focus = GRE_open_up_the_country
            NOT = { has_global_flag = GRE_crete_still_holding }
            NOT = { has_global_flag = GRE_government_in_exile }
            has_appropriate_materiel_mot_fm_selected = yes
		}
        
        days_remove = 14
        cost = 25

		remove_effect = {
            #####################[Domestic Competition Limits]####################
            if = {
                limit = { has_idea = GRE_domestic_competition_0_hidden }
                set_temp_variable = { bonus_from_domcom_level = 0.60 }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = { has_idea = GRE_domestic_competition_1_hidden }
                set_temp_variable = { bonus_from_domcom_level = 0.40 }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = { has_idea = GRE_domestic_competition_2_hidden }
                set_temp_variable = { bonus_from_domcom_level = 0.10 }
            }
            else = {
                set_temp_variable = { bonus_from_domcom_level = 0.00 }
            }
            ########################[FROM Has Tech Bonus]########################
            if = {
                limit = { 
                    FROM = {
                        meta_trigger = {
                            text = { has_tech = [ITEM] }
                            ITEM = "[GRE.GetNextTruck]"
                        }
                    }
                }
                set_temp_variable = { bonus_from_researched_tech = 0.4 }
            }
            else = {
                set_temp_variable = { bonus_from_researched_tech = 0.1 }
            }
            ##########################[Country Bonuses]##########################
            if = { 
                limit = { FROM = { original_tag = JAP } }
                set_temp_variable = { bonus_from_country = 0.12 }
            }
            else_if = { 
                limit = { FROM = { original_tag = ITA } }
                set_temp_variable = { bonus_from_country = 0.12 }
            }
            add_bonuses_to_sum = yes
            meta_effect = {
                text = { add_tech_bonus = { name=GRE_FM_mot_bonus bonus=[BONUS_SUM] uses=1 technology=[ITEM] } }
                BONUS_SUM = "[?sum|.3]"
                ITEM = "[GRE.GetNextTruck]"
            }
        }
    }

    GRE_foreign_manufacturer_industry_investments = {
        on_map_mode = map_and_decisions_view
        highlight_states = { highlight_states_trigger = { state = FROM.capital } }
        
        icon = generic_industry
		allowed = { tag = GRE }
        priority = 12
        days_re_enable = 550

		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
                OR = {
                    original_tag = GER 
                    original_tag = SOV 
                }
			}
		}

		available = {
			date < 1942.1.1
            FROM = { exists = yes }
			NOT = {
				has_war_with = FROM
                custom_trigger_tooltip = {
                    tooltip = GRE_favor_abysmal_from_tt
                    check_variable = { var = FROM.favor@GRE value = 0 compare = less_than }
                }
			}
            has_completed_appropriate_fm_focuses = yes
		}
        
		visible = {
            NOT = { has_country_flag = toggle_fm }
			has_completed_focus = GRE_open_up_the_country
            NOT = { has_global_flag = GRE_crete_still_holding }
            NOT = { has_global_flag = GRE_government_in_exile }
            has_appropriate_industrial_fm_selected = yes  
		}
        
        days_remove = 14
        cost = 25

		remove_effect = {
            #####################[Domestic Competition Limits]####################
            if = {
                limit = { has_idea = GRE_domestic_competition_0_hidden }
                set_temp_variable = { bonus_from_domcom_level = 0.00 }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = { has_idea = GRE_domestic_competition_1_hidden }
                set_temp_variable = { bonus_from_domcom_level = 0.00 }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = { has_idea = GRE_domestic_competition_2_hidden }
                set_temp_variable = { bonus_from_domcom_level = 0.00 }
            }
            else = {
                set_temp_variable = { bonus_from_domcom_level = 0.00 }
            }
            ########################[FROM Has Tech Bonus]########################
            if = {
                limit = { 
                    OR = {
                        AND = {
                            GRE = {
                                NOT = { has_tech = concentrated_industry }
                                NOT = { has_tech = dispersed_industry }
                            }
                            FROM = {
                                OR = {
                                    has_tech = concentrated_industry
                                    has_tech = dispersed_industry
                                }
                            }
                        }
                        AND = {
                            GRE = { OR = { has_tech = concentrated_industry has_tech = dispersed_industry} }
                            meta_trigger = {
                                text = { FROM = { has_tech = [ITEM ] } }
                                ITEM = "[GRE.GetNextIndustry]"
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                set_temp_variable = { bonus_from_researched_tech = 0.4 }
            }
            else = {
                set_temp_variable = { bonus_from_researched_tech = 0.1 }
            }
            ##########################[Country Bonuses]##########################
            if = { 
                limit = { FROM = { original_tag = GER } }
                set_temp_variable = { bonus_from_country = 0.10 }
            }
            else_if = { 
                limit = { FROM = { original_tag = SOV } }
                set_temp_variable = { bonus_from_country = 0.10 }
            }
            add_bonuses_to_sum = yes
            if = { 
                limit = { NOT = { has_tech = concentrated_industry } NOT = { has_tech = dispersed_industry } FROM = { has_tech = concentrated_industry } }
                meta_effect = {
                    text = { add_tech_bonus = { name=GRE_FM_industrial_bonus bonus=[BONUS_SUM] uses=1 technology=[ITEM] } }
                    BONUS_SUM = "[?sum|.3]"
                    ITEM = "concentrated_industry"
                }
            }
            else_if = { 
                limit = { NOT = { has_tech = concentrated_industry } NOT = { has_tech = dispersed_industry } FROM = { has_tech = dispersed_industry } }
                meta_effect = {
                    text = { add_tech_bonus = { name=GRE_FM_industrial_bonus bonus=[BONUS_SUM] uses=1 technology=[ITEM] } }
                    BONUS_SUM = "[?sum|.3]"
                    ITEM = "dispersed_industry"
                }
            }
            else = {
                meta_effect = {
                    text = { add_tech_bonus = { name=GRE_FM_industrial_bonus bonus=[BONUS_SUM] uses=1 technology=[ITEM] } }
                    BONUS_SUM = "[?sum|.3]"
                    ITEM = "[GRE.GetNextIndustry]"
                }
            }
        }
    }

                    FROM = {
                        meta_trigger = {
                            text = { has_tech = [ITEM] }
                            ITEM = "[GRE.GetNextRadar]"
                        }
                    }
                }
                set_temp_variable = { bonus_from_researched_tech = 0.4 }
            }
            else = {
                set_temp_variable = { bonus_from_researched_tech = 0.1 }
            }
            ##########################[Country Bonuses]##########################
            if = { 
                limit = { FROM = { original_tag = GER } }
                set_temp_variable = { bonus_from_country = 0.12 }
            }
            else_if = { 
                limit = { FROM = { original_tag = USA } }
                set_temp_variable = { bonus_from_country = 0.12 }
            }
            else_if = { 
                limit = { FROM = { original_tag = ENG } }
                set_temp_variable = { bonus_from_country = 0.12 }
            }
            add_bonuses_to_sum = yes
            meta_effect = {
                text = { add_tech_bonus = { name=GRE_FM_industrial_bonus bonus=[BONUS_SUM] uses=1 technology=[ITEM] } }
                BONUS_SUM = "[?sum|.3]"
                ITEM = "[GRE.GetNextRadar]"
            }
        }
    }

    GRE_foreign_manufacturer_electric_investments = {
        on_map_mode = map_and_decisions_view
        highlight_states = { highlight_states_trigger = { state = FROM.capital } }
        
        icon = generic_industry
		allowed = { tag = GRE }
        priority = 12
        days_re_enable = 550

		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
                OR = {
                    original_tag = GER 
                    original_tag = ENG 
                    original_tag = USA 
                }
			}
		}

		available = {
			date < 1942.1.1
            FROM = { exists = yes }
			NOT = {
				has_war_with = FROM
                custom_trigger_tooltip = {
                    tooltip = GRE_favor_abysmal_from_tt
                    check_variable = { var = FROM.favor@GRE value = 0 compare = less_than }
                }
			}
            has_completed_appropriate_fm_focuses = yes
		}
        
		visible = {
            NOT = { has_country_flag = toggle_fm }
			has_completed_focus = GRE_open_up_the_country
            NOT = { has_global_flag = GRE_crete_still_holding }
            NOT = { has_global_flag = GRE_government_in_exile }
            has_appropriate_electrical_fm_selected = yes  
		}
        
        days_remove = 14
        cost = 25

		remove_effect = {
            #####################[Domestic Competition Limits]####################
            if = {
                limit = { has_idea = GRE_domestic_competition_0_hidden }
                set_temp_variable = { bonus_from_domcom_level = 0.00 }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = { has_idea = GRE_domestic_competition_1_hidden }
                set_temp_variable = { bonus_from_domcom_level = 0.00 }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = { has_idea = GRE_domestic_competition_2_hidden }
                set_temp_variable = { bonus_from_domcom_level = 0.00 }
            }
            else = {
                set_temp_variable = { bonus_from_domcom_level = 0.00 }
            }
            ########################[FROM Has Tech Bonus]########################
            if = {
                limit = { 
                    FROM = {
                        meta_trigger = {
                            text = { has_tech = [ITEM] }
                            ITEM = "[GRE.GetNextMechEng]"
                        }
                    }
                }
                set_temp_variable = { bonus_from_researched_tech = 0.4 }
            }
            else = {
                set_temp_variable = { bonus_from_researched_tech = 0.1 }
            }
            ##########################[Country Bonuses]##########################
            if = { 
                limit = { FROM = { original_tag = GER } }
                set_temp_variable = { bonus_from_country = 0.12 }
            }
            else_if = { 
                limit = { FROM = { original_tag = USA } }
                set_temp_variable = { bonus_from_country = 0.12 }
            }
            else_if = { 
                limit = { FROM = { original_tag = ENG } }
                set_temp_variable = { bonus_from_country = 0.12 }
            }
            add_bonuses_to_sum = yes
            meta_effect = {

    GRE_choosing_a_lignite_partner = {
        icon = oil
        allowed = { tag = GRE }
        highlight_states = { highlight_states_trigger = { state = FROM.capital } }

        available = {
            has_country_flag = GRE_debt_free
            FROM = { has_opinion = { target = GRE value > 60 } }
        }

        targets = { ENG USA SOV GER }
		target_root_trigger = {
			has_completed_focus = GRE_lignite_liquefaction
		}

        visible = {
            has_completed_focus = GRE_open_up_the_country
            NOT = { has_country_flag = GRE_has_partner_lignite }
            NOT = { has_country_flag = toggle_adio }
        }

        cost = 75
        fire_only_once = yes
        days_remove = 14

        complete_effect = { set_country_flag = GRE_has_partner_lignite }
        
        remove_effect = {
            if = {
                limit = { FROM = { belongs_in_the_allied_sphere = yes } }
                set_temp_variable = { tmpT = 0 }
                set_temp_variable = { tmpQ = 8 }
                tmpT_axal_by_tmpQ = yes
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = { FROM = { belongs_in_the_axis_sphere = yes } }
                set_temp_variable = { tmpT = 1 }
                set_temp_variable = { tmpQ = 8 }
                tmpT_axal_by_tmpQ = yes
            }
            set_temp_variable = { findX = FROM.id }
            set_temp_variable = { findY = 6 }
            custom_effect_tooltip = favor_boost_with_findX_by_findY  
            add_to_variable = { FROM.favor@GRE = findY }
            FROM = {
                random_core_state = {
                    add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
                    add_building_construction = {
                        type = synthetic_refinery
                        level = 2
                        instant_build = yes
                    }
                }
            }
            random_owned_controlled_state = {
				prioritize = { 186 }
               	limit = {
                    free_building_slots = {
                       	building = synthetic_refinery
                        size > 0
                        include_locked = yes
                    }
                }
                add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
                add_building_construction = {
                    type = synthetic_refinery
                    level = 2
                    instant_build = yes
                }
            }
            set_variable = { GRE_lignite_partner = FROM.id }
        }
    }

    GRE_recommission_the_american_battleships = {
		
		icon = generic_naval
        on_map_mode = map_and_decisions_view
        highlight_states = { highlight_states_trigger = { state = 47 } }

		allowed = { 
			tag = GRE
			has_dlc = "Battle for the Bosporus"
		}

		available = {
			NOT = { has_war_with = USA }
			has_completed_focus = GRE_american_influencers
            has_completed_focus = GRE_the_navy
		}

		cost = 0

		fire_only_once = yes

		visible = {
            has_completed_focus = GRE_open_up_the_country
            has_completed_focus = GRE_american_influencers
            NOT = { has_war_with = USA }
            hidden_trigger = {
                NOT = { 
                    has_global_flag = GRE_crete_still_holding 
                    has_global_flag = GRE_government_in_exile
                    has_country_flag = toggle_adio 
                }
            }
		}

		cancel_if_not_visible = yes

		complete_effect = {
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					NOT = { has_dlc = "Man the Guns" }
				}
				add_equipment_production = {
					equipment = {
						type = battleship_1
					}
					requested_factories = 1
					progress = 0.8
					amount = 1
				}
				add_equipment_production = {
					equipment = {
						type = battleship_1
					}
					requested_factories = 1
					progress = 0.75
					amount = 1
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { 
					has_dlc = "Man the Guns"
				}
				hidden_effect = { 
					create_equipment_variant = {
						name = "Mississippi Class"
						type = ship_hull_heavy_1
						name_group = GRE_BB_HISTORICAL
						parent_version = 0
						modules = { 
							fixed_ship_battery_slot = ship_heavy_battery_2
							fixed_ship_anti_air_slot = ship_anti_air_1

            }

		}

		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
                OR = {
                    original_tag = ENG
                    original_tag = GER
                }
			}
		}

		cost = 0
        days_remove = 730

		fire_only_once = no

		visible = {
            has_completed_focus = GRE_buy_subs
            has_completed_focus = GRE_open_up_the_country
            NOT = { has_global_flag = GRE_crete_still_holding }
            NOT = { has_global_flag = GRE_government_in_exile }
            NOT = { 
                has_country_flag = subs_ordered 
                has_country_flag = toggle_adio
            }
		}
        
        complete_effect = {
            set_country_flag = subs_ordered
            add_to_variable = { FROM.favor@GRE = 5 }
            custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_favor_boost_mediocre_from_tt
        }
        remove_effect = {
            if = {
                limit = {
                    FROM = { original_tag = GER }
                } 
                create_equipment_variant = {
                    name = "U-boat Class"
                    type = ship_hull_submarine_3
                    name_group = GRE_SS_HISTORICAL
                    parent_version = 0
                    modules = {
                        fixed_ship_torpedo_slot = ship_torpedo_sub_3
                        mid_1_custom_slot = ship_sub_snorkel_1
                        fixed_ship_engine_slot = sub_ship_engine_3
                        rear_1_custom_slot = ship_torpedo_sub_3
                    }
                }
                if = { 
                    limit = {
                        GER = { NOT = { has_war_with = ENG } }
                    }              
                    resize_array = { ship_builder = 12 }                ## Tell it to build 12 ships
                }
                else = {
                    resize_array = { ship_builder = 6 }                 ## Tell it to build  6 ships
                }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    FROM = { original_tag = ENG }
                } 
                create_equipment_variant = {
                    name = "Undine Class"
                    type = ship_hull_submarine_3
                    name_group = GRE_SS_HISTORICAL
                    parent_version = 0
                    modules = {
                        fixed_ship_torpedo_slot = ship_torpedo_sub_3
                        mid_1_custom_slot = ship_sub_snorkel_1
                        fixed_ship_engine_slot = sub_ship_engine_3
                        rear_1_custom_slot = ship_torpedo_sub_3
                    }
                }
                if = { 
                    limit = {
                        GER = { NOT = { has_war_with = ENG } }
                    }
                    resize_array = { ship_builder = 12 }                ## Tell it to build 12 ships
                }
                else = {
                    resize_array = { ship_builder = 6 }                 ## Tell it to build  6 ships
                }
            }
            spawn_subs = yes                                            ### -> Scripted effect
        }
    }

                tooltip = GRE_favor_at_least_mediocre_from_tt
                check_variable = { FROM.favor@GRE > 29 }
            }
            NOT = { has_war_with = FROM }
		}

		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
                OR = {
                    original_tag = ENG
                    original_tag = USA
                    original_tag = GER
                    original_tag = FRA
                    original_tag = SOV
                }
			}
		}

		cost = 75
        days_remove = 30

		fire_only_once = yes

		visible = {
            has_completed_focus = GRE_open_up_the_country
            has_completed_focus = GRE_seek_additional_deals
            NOT = { has_global_flag = GRE_crete_still_holding }
            NOT = { has_global_flag = GRE_government_in_exile }
            NOT = {
                has_country_flag = weaps_ordered
                has_country_flag = toggle_adio
            }
		}
        
        complete_effect = {
            set_country_flag = weaps_ordered
            subtract_from_variable = { GRE_budget_choices = 1 }
        }
        
        remove_effect = {
            set_temp_variable = { x = 1000 }
            if = { 
                limit = { check_variable = { FROM.favor@GRE > 79 } }
                multiply_temp_variable = { x = 3 }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = { check_variable = { FROM.favor@GRE > 49 } }
                multiply_temp_variable = { x = 2 }
            }
            add_to_temp_variable = { x = 5000 }
            add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment_1 amount = x producer = FROM }
        }
    }

    GRE_fundraising_an_airforce = {

		icon = generic_air

		allowed = { tag=GRE }

		cost = 25
        days_remove = 30

		fire_only_once = yes

		visible = {
            has_completed_focus = GRE_open_up_the_country
            has_completed_focus = GRE_fundraising_an_airforce
            NOT = { has_global_flag = GRE_crete_still_holding }
            NOT = { has_global_flag = GRE_government_in_exile }
            NOT = {
                has_country_flag = airforce_funded
                has_country_flag = toggle_adio
            }
		}
        
        complete_effect = {
            set_country_flag = airforce_funded
            custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_fundraising_an_airforce_tt
        }
        
        remove_effect = {
            if = { 
                limit = { NOT = { has_completed_focus = GRE_dreams_of_a_grand_coalition } }
                if = {
                    limit = {                                                                           ## If all factions are friendly
                        check_variable = { fct_com > 70 }
                        check_variable = { fct_mon > 70 }
                        check_variable = { fct_dem > 70 }
                        check_variable = { fct_fas > 70 }
                    }
                    if = {
                        limit = { has_tech = fighter3 }
                        add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = fighter_equipment_3 amount = 48 producer = GRE }
                    }
                    else_if = {
                        limit = { has_tech = fighter2 }
                        add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = fighter_equipment_2 amount = 48 producer = GRE }
                    }
                    else_if = {
                        limit = { has_tech = fighter1 }
                        add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = fighter_equipment_1 amount = 48 producer = GRE }
                    }
                    if = {
                        limit = { has_tech = CAS3 }
                        add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = CAS_equipment_3 amount = 36 producer = GRE }
                    }
                    else_if = {
                        limit = { has_tech = CAS2 }
                        add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = CAS_equipment_2 amount = 36 producer = GRE }
                    }
                    else_if = {
                        limit = { has_tech = CAS1 }
                        add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = CAS_equipment_1 amount = 36 producer = GRE }
                    }
                    if = {
                        limit = { has_tech = naval_bomber3 }
                        add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = nav_bomber_equipment_3 amount = 36 producer = GRE }
                    }
                    else_if = {
                        limit = { has_tech = naval_bomber2 }
                        add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = nav_bomber_equipment_2 amount = 36 producer = GRE }
                    }
                    else_if = {
                        limit = { has_tech = naval_bomber1 }
                        add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = nav_bomber_equipment_1 amount = 36 producer = GRE }
                    }
                    if = {
                        limit = { has_tech = tactical_bomber3 }
                        add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = tac_bomber_equipment_3 amount = 48 producer = GRE }
                    }
                    else_if = {
                        limit = { has_tech = tactical_bomber2 }
                        add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = tac_bomber_equipment_2 amount = 48 producer = GRE }
                    }
                    else_if = {
                        limit = { has_tech = tactical_bomber1 }

#GREECE DEBT DECISIONS
GRE_economic_alleviation_category = { 

	## Missions base: 365 (*10 = 3650)
	## Stability subtracts up to 100 days from base. Linearly. Gets us to 265.
    ## Each Metaxas' projects subtracts 5 from base apart from reducing current. If 30 total, then 150 days off. Gets us to 115.
    ## Each MEtaxas' Propaganda subtracts 10 from base apart from reducing current. If 10 total, then 100 days off. Gets us to 15.

    invigorating_hellenic_spirit = {
		icon=begging
        highlight_states = { highlight_state_targets={ state=47 }}

		allowed = { tag=GRE }
		activation = { has_completed_focus=GRE_utilize_our_strengths check_variable={ GRE.invigorating_level<1 }}
        available = { hidden_trigger={ always=no }}

		days_mission_timeout=365
		fire_only_once=no
		is_good = yes

		timeout_effect = {
            add_to_variable = { GRE.invigorating_level=0.1 tooltip=invigorating_towards_completion_tt}
            add_to_variable = { gre_agr_mp = 0.150 }
            add_to_variable = { gre_agr_cf = 0.050 }
            add_to_variable = { gre_agr_stbw = 0.001 }
            custom_effect_tooltip = gre_mis_agr_increase_tt
            hidden_effect = {
                if = {
                    limit={ check_variable={ GRE.invigorating_level=1 }}
                    remove_dynamic_modifier={ modifier=GRE_agrarian_society_dyn }
                    add_ideas=GRE_farmer_culture
                    if = {
                        limit = { check_variable={ GRE.working_level=1 }}
                        improve_tied_economy_spirit = yes
                    }
                }
                else = {
                    activate_mission=invigorating_hellenic_spirit
                    47 = { state_event = { id = hellas.33 days=0 random=4 } }
                }
            }
		}
    }

    workers_entering_factories = {
		icon=industry
        highlight_states = { highlight_state_targets={ state=47 }}

		allowed = { tag=GRE }
		activation = { has_completed_focus=GRE_force_the_farmers_into_factories check_variable={ GRE.working_level<1 }}
        available = { hidden_trigger={ always=no }}

		days_mission_timeout=365
		fire_only_once=no
		is_good = yes

		timeout_effect = {
            add_to_variable = { GRE.working_level=0.1 tooltip=working_towards_completion_tt}
            add_to_variable = { gre_noi_gbs = 0.075 }
            add_to_variable = { gre_noi_pfegf = 0.01 }
            add_to_variable = { gre_noi_pfmef = 0.005 }
            add_to_variable = { gre_noi_icd = 0.08 }
            add_to_variable = { gre_noi_icf = 0.08 }
            add_to_variable = { gre_noi_irf = 0.05 }
            add_to_variable = { gre_noi_stbw = 0.001 }
            
            custom_effect_tooltip = gre_mis_ind_increase_tt
            hidden_effect = {
                if = {
                    limit={ check_variable={ GRE.working_level=1 }}
                    remove_dynamic_modifier={ modifier=GRE_no_industrilization_dyn }
                    add_ideas=GRE_industrializing_society    
                    if = {
                        limit = { check_variable={ GRE.working_level=1 }}
                        improve_tied_economy_spirit = yes
                    }
                }
                else = {
                    activate_mission=workers_entering_factories
                    913 = { state_event = { id = hellas.33 days=0 random=4 } }
                }
            }
		}
    }

            }
            else_if = {
                limit = { has_idea=GRE_spent_too_much }

                has_army_experience > 149.99
                has_country_flag = GRE_victor_in_a_war   
                NOT = { has_idea = GRE_army_leadership_0 }

                limit = { check_variable={ var=GRE_ges value=2 compare=greater_than_or_equals }}

		icon = geetha
        state_target = yes
        on_map_mode = map_and_decisions_view

        }

            calculate_schachtplan_decision_costs=yes
            ###[Germany Effects]###
            if = { limit={ has_idea=GRE_schachtplan } set_temp_variable={ fout=-0.03 }}
            else_if = { limit={ has_idea=GRE_schachtplan_modified } set_temp_variable={ fout=-0.04 }}
            else_if = { limit={ has_idea=GRE_schachtplan_stabilized } set_temp_variable={ fout=-0.05 }}
            multiply_temp_variable={ gerpp?0.5=GRE.schachtplan_cost }
            GER={
                add_political_power = gerpp
                set_variable={ GER.gap_fout=fout }
                add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier=GRE_greek_armament_purchases days=7 }
                custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_greek_subsidized_factories_cost_tt
            }
            ###[AXAL MECHANIC]###
            set_temp_variable = { tmpQ=0.75 }
            custom_effect_tooltip = axal_increase_by_tmpQ
            add_to_variable = { GRE.axal = tmpQ }
            axal_gui_call = yes
        }
            
		remove_effect = {
            if = {
                limit = { has_idea=GRE_schachtplan }
                add_equipment_to_stockpile={ type=infantry_equipment amount=500 producer=GER }
                add_equipment_to_stockpile={ type=support_equipment amount=20 producer=GER }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = { has_idea=GRE_schachtplan_modified }
                add_equipment_to_stockpile={ type=infantry_equipment amount=550 producer=GER }
                add_equipment_to_stockpile={ type=support_equipment amount=30 producer=GER }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = { has_idea=GRE_schachtplan_stabilized }
                add_equipment_to_stockpile={ type=infantry_equipment amount=600 producer=GER }
                add_equipment_to_stockpile={ type=support_equipment amount=40 producer=GER }
            }
            custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_utilize_schlachtplan_tt
		}
    }

    GRE_conduct_exercises_serres_mis= {
		icon = infil
		allowed = { tag = GRE }
        highlight_states = { highlight_states_trigger = { state = 914 } }
        activation = { always = no }    

		available = {
            army_manpower_in_state = {
                state = 914
                amount < 6000
            }
        }

        is_good = yes
        days_mission_timeout = 14
        fixed_random_seed = no
        
        timeout_effect = {
            clr_country_flag = conducting_exercises_serres_mil
            set_temp_variable = { indX = 4 }
            custom_effect_tooltip = train_up_to_indX_officers_in_exercise_tt
            custom_effect_tooltip = train_assigned_generals_disclaimer_tt
            hidden_effect = {
                resize_temp_array = { general_quotas = indX }
                for_each_loop = {
                    array = general_quotas
                    
                    if = {
                        limit = { 
                            any_army_leader = { 
                                assigned_has_unpreparedness_level = yes 
                                not_recently_trained = yes 
                                check_variable = { num_units_in_state@914:id > 1 } 
                            }
                        }
                        random_army_leader = {
                            limit = { assigned_has_unpreparedness_level = yes not_recently_trained = yes  check_variable = { num_units_in_state@914:id > 1 } }
                            reduce_unpreparedness = yes
                        }
                    }
                    else = {
                        random_army_leader = {
                            limit = { has_unpreparedness_level = yes not_recently_trained = yes }
                            reduce_unpreparedness = yes
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        
        complete_effect = {
            army_experience = 2
            clr_country_flag = conducting_exercises_serres_mil
        }
    }

                    every_army_leader = {
                        if = {
                            limit = { has_trait = gre_unprepared_general_3 }
                            add_to_temp_variable = { lvl3_unprepared_generals = 1 }
                        }
                        else_if = {
                            limit = { has_trait = gre_unprepared_general_2 }
                            add_to_temp_variable = { lvl2_unprepared_generals = 1 }
                        }
                        else_if = {
                            limit = { has_trait = gre_unprepared_general_1 }
                            add_to_temp_variable = { lvl1_unprepared_generals = 1 }
                        }
                        else_if = {
                            limit = { has_trait = gre_unprepared_general_0 }
                            add_to_temp_variable = { lvl1_unprepared_generals = 1 }
                        }
                    }
                    #########################################################
                    set_temp_variable = { indX = lvl3_unprepared_generals }
                    set_temp_variable = { indY = 0.15 }
                    multiply_temp_variable = { indX = indY }
                    round_temp_variable = indX
                    set_temp_variable = { tmpX = indX }
                    set_temp_variable = { tmpY = 0 }
                    randomly_train_tmpX_officers = yes
                    ##########################################################
                    set_temp_variable = { indX = lvl2_unprepared_generals }
                    set_temp_variable = { indY = 0.10 }
                    multiply_temp_variable = { indX = indY }
                    round_temp_variable = indX
                    set_temp_variable = { tmpX = indX }
                    set_temp_variable = { tmpY = 0 }
                    randomly_train_tmpX_officers = yes
                    ##########################################################
                }
                if = { 
                    limit = { any_army_leader = { has_trait = gre_unprepared_general_0 not_recently_trained = yes } }
                    random_army_leader = {
                        limit = { has_trait = gre_unprepared_general_0 not_recently_trained = yes }
                        reduce_unpreparedness = yes
                    }
                }
                resize_temp_array = { lvlups_array = 2 }
                for_each_loop = {
                    array = lvlups_array
                
                    if = {
                        limit = { any_army_leader = { has_trait = gre_unprepared_general_1 not_recently_trained = yes } }
                        random_army_leader = {
                            limit = { has_trait = gre_unprepared_general_1 not_recently_trained = yes }
                            reduce_unpreparedness = yes
                        }
                    }                    
                }
            }
        }
    }

GRE_the_eastern_prospect_category = {

	

    GRE_send_additional_equipment_over_ep = {
        on_map_mode = map_and_decisions_view
        highlight_states = { highlight_states_trigger = { state = FROM.capital } }                 ### CHECK IF BOTH FAVOR AND THIS WORK PROPERLY AS THEY BOTH TARGET CAPITAL (IF BOTH SHOW)
		icon = generic_army_support

		allowed = { tag=GRE }
		available = { 
            NOT = { has_war_with = FROM }
            if = { limit={ FROM={ original_tag=CHI }} has_completed_focus = GRE_extend_arms_sales_to_the_chinese }
            else_if = { limit={ FROM={ original_tag=JAP }} has_completed_focus = GRE_arm_the_japanese } 
            else_if = { limit={ FROM={ original_tag=PRC }} has_completed_focus = GRE_arm_the_communists }
            has_equipment = { infantry_equipment>249 }
            has_equipment = { support_equipment>24 }
		}

        targets = { YUN SIK GXC SHX XSM CHI PRC JAP MEN MAN }

		fire_only_once = no
        days_remove = 14
		visible = {
            OR = {
                has_completed_focus=GRE_extend_arms_sales_to_the_chinese
                has_completed_focus=GRE_arm_the_japanese
                has_completed_focus=GRE_arm_the_communists
            }
            FROM = {
                exists=yes
                if = { limit={ NOT={ OR={ original_tag=JAP original_tag=MEN original_tag=MAN }}} has_war_with=JAP }
                else = { OR={ has_war_with=CHI has_war_with=PRC }}
            }
		}
        
        complete_effect = {
            #custom_effect_tooltip = ep_extend_arms_deal_FROM
            army_experience = 2.00
            hidden_effect = {
                send_equipment = {
                    equipment = infantry_equipment
                    amount = 250
                    target = FROM
                }
                send_equipment = {
                    equipment = support_equipment_1
                    amount = 25
                    target = FROM
                }    
            } 
            FROM = {
                custom_effect_tooltip = sija_saeo_tt
                set_temp_variable = { findX=THIS.id }
                set_temp_variable = { findY=5 }
                add_to_variable = { findX.favor@GRE=findY tooltip=favor_boost_with_findX_by_findY_no_name_tt }
            }
            every_country = {
                limit = { is_in_faction_with=FROM NOT={ original_tag=FROM }}
                set_temp_variable = { findX=THIS.id }
                set_temp_variable = { findY=2.5 }
                add_to_variable = { findX.favor@GRE=findY tooltip=favor_boost_with_findX_by_findY_no_name_tt }
            }
            every_country = { 
                limit = { has_war_with=FROM }
                set_temp_variable = { findX=THIS.id }
                set_temp_variable = { findY=-2 }
                add_to_variable = { findX.favor@GRE=findY tooltip=favor_hit_with_findX_by_findY_no_name_tt }
            }
            if = {
                limit = { threat>0.21 FROM={ OR={ tag=CHI tag=JAP tag=PRC }}}
                custom_effect_tooltip = sija_tension_problems_tt
                every_country = {
                    limit = {
                        NOT = { tag=JAP tag=CHI tag=PRC }
                        is_major=yes
                        if = { limit={ FROM={ original_tag=CHI }} OR={ has_government=neutrality has_government=democratic }}
                        else_if = { limit={ FROM={ original_tag=JAP }} has_government=fascism }
                        else = { has_government=communism }
                    }
                    set_temp_variable = { findX=THIS.id }
                    set_temp_variable_to_random = { var=findY min=1 max=2 }
                    add_to_variable = { THIS.favor@GRE=findY tooltip=favor_boost_with_findX_by_findY_no_name_tt }
                }
                every_country = {
                    limit = {
                        NOT = { tag=JAP tag=CHI tag=PRC }
                        is_major=yes
                        if = { limit={ FROM={ original_tag=CHI }} has_government=fascism }
                        else_if = { limit={ FROM={ original_tag=JAP }} NOT={ has_government=fascism }}
                        else = { has_government=fascism }
                    }
                    set_temp_variable = { findX=THIS.id }
                    set_temp_variable_to_random = { var=findY min=-4 max=-2 }
                    add_to_variable = { THIS.favor@GRE=findY tooltip=favor_hit_with_findX_by_findY_no_name_tt }
                }
            }
            custom_effect_tooltip="                                      "
        }
            
		remove_effect = {
            add_to_variable = { GRE.gold_reserves=0.5 tooltip=increase_gold_reserves_tt}
            if = {
                limit = { any_character={ is_character=GRE_prodromos_bodosakis check_variable={ trait_level<7 }}}

                add_to_variable={ GRE.bodosakis_experience=15 tooltip=bodosakis_experience_tt }
                calculate_bodosakis_experience_for_upgrade=yes
            }
            recalculate_gold_reserve_bonuses=yes
		}
    }

    ep_speak_in_favor_FROM = {
		icon = deals
        on_map_mode = map_and_decisions_view
        highlight_states = { highlight_states_trigger = { state = FROM.capital } }
		allowed = { original_tag = GRE }
        targets = { JAP CHI PRC }
		cost = 0
        days_remove = 60

		fire_only_once = yes

		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = GRE_extend_arms_sales_to_the_chinese
            has_completed_focus = GRE_arm_the_japanese
            has_completed_focus = GRE_arm_the_communists
		}
        
		available = {
            NOT = { has_war_with = FROM }
            set_temp_variable = { tmpQ = 49 }
            custom_trigger_tooltip = {
                tooltip = ep_from_leading_alignment_by_tmpQ_tt
                check_variable = { GRE.ep_perc@FROM > tmpQ }
            }
        }
        
        complete_effect = {}
		remove_effect = {}
    }
}

GRE_grecoitalian_war_category = {

    GRE_stabilize_the_line = {

		icon = border_war
        #on_map_mode = map_and_decisions_view
        highlight_states = {
 			highlight_state_targets = { 
                state = 185
            }
		}


		allowed = { tag=GRE }

		activation = {
            has_country_flag = GRE_hidden_flag
		}        

		available = { 
            custom_trigger_tooltip = {
                tooltip = GRE_stabilized_the_line_tt
                OR = {
                    check_variable = { var = global.province_controllers^9916 value = ITA compare = equals }
                    check_variable = { var = global.province_controllers^3914 value = ITA compare = equals }
                    check_variable = { var = global.province_controllers^3980 value = ITA compare = equals }
                    check_variable = { var = global.province_controllers^966 value = ITA compare = equals }
                    check_variable = { var = global.province_controllers^936 value = ITA compare = equals }
                }
            }
		}

		days_mission_timeout = 16

		fire_only_once = yes

		visible = {
            has_country_flag = GRE_hidden_flag
		}

		cancel_if_not_visible = no

		is_good = yes

		complete_effect = { 
            news_event = { id = hellenic_news.150 days = 0 }                               ### News report event: Italians blast through greek defences.
            hidden_effect = { 
                set_country_flag = GRE_italian_breakthrough 
                ITA = { news_event = { id = hellenic_news.150 days = 0 } }
            } 
		}

		timeout_effect = {
            news_event = { id = hellenic_news.151 days = 0 }                               ### News report event: Greeks hold the Italians back.
            if = {
                limit = {
                    NOT = { has_completed_focus = GRE_stabilizing_the_line }
                }
                complete_national_focus = GRE_stabilizing_the_line
            }
            hidden_effect = { 
                ITA = { news_event = { id = hellenic_news.151 days = 0 } }
                set_country_flag = GRE_italian_advance_halted                              ### Set flag (to allow counter-offensive).  
                activate_decision = the_winter_counter_offensive                           ## Automatically begin counter offensive to avoid cheese tactics by player. To be determined.
                activate_mission = GRE_winter_counter_offensive
            }              
		}    
    
    }
    
    GRE_stabilize_the_line_2 = {

		allowed = { tag=GRE }

            }

		}

		timeout_effect = {
            news_event = { id = hellenic_news.151 days = 0 }                               ### News report event: Greeks hold the Italians back.

GRE_economic_fluidity = {

    GRE_expand_collapse_tariff_decisions = {
        icon = decision_generic_decision
    
        allowed = { tag=GRE }
        
        fire_only_once = no
        days_remove = 0
        days_re_enable = 0
        priority = 12
        
        visible = {
            has_completed_focus = GRE_tariff
            NOT = { has_global_flag = GRE_grecoitalian_start }
            NOT = { has_global_flag = GRE_crete_still_holding }
            NOT = { has_global_flag = GRE_government_in_exile }
        }
        
        complete_effect = {
            hidden_effect = {
                if = {
                    limit = {
                        NOT = { has_country_flag = toggle_tariff }
                    }
                    set_country_flag = toggle_tariff
                }
                else = {
                    clr_country_flag = toggle_tariff
                }
            }
        }
    }

    impose_tarrifs = {
    
		icon = tariff

		allowed = { tag=GRE }

		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
                is_in_array = {
                    array = global.favor_mechanic
                    value = THIS.id
                }          
			}
		}
        
        available = {
            has_country_flag = GRE_debt_free
        }
        
        available = {
            has_completed_focus = GRE_open_foreign_subsidized_factories
            has_completed_focus = GRE_bedrock_of_balkan_financial_stability
            has_completed_focus = GRE_economic_fluidity_plans
        }
        
        visible = {
            has_completed_focus = GRE_tariff
            if = {
                limit = {
                    FROM = { is_major = no }
                }
                check_variable = { FROM.favor@GRE > 49 }
            }
            FROM = { NOT = { has_idea = GRtar_trade_3 } }
            NOT = { has_country_flag = toggle_tariff }
            NOT = { has_global_flag = GRE_grecoitalian_start }
            NOT = { has_global_flag = GRE_crete_still_holding }
            NOT = { has_global_flag = GRE_government_in_exile }
        }

        cost = 50

		fire_only_once = no

		days_remove = 0

		complete_effect = {
            FROM = { 
                if = {
                    limit = {
                        has_idea = GRtar_trade_2
                    }
                    swap_ideas = {
                        remove_idea = GRtar_trade_2
                        add_idea = GRtar_trade_3
                    }
                    set_variable = { GRE.tariff_level@FROM = 3 }
                }
                else_if = {
                    limit = {
                        has_idea = GRtar_trade_1
                    }
                    swap_ideas = {
                        remove_idea = GRtar_trade_1
                        add_idea = GRtar_trade_2
                    }
                    set_variable = { GRE.tariff_level@FROM = 2 }
                }
                else = {
                    add_ideas = GRtar_trade_1
                    set_variable = { GRE.tariff_level@FROM = 1 }
                }
            }
		}    
    }
    
    reduce_tariffs = {
    
		icon = tariff

		allowed = { tag=GRE }

		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
                is_in_array = {
                    array = global.favor_mechanic
                    value = THIS.id
                }          
			}
		}
        
        available = {
            has_country_flag = GRE_debt_free
        }
        
        available = {
            has_completed_focus = GRE_open_foreign_subsidized_factories
            has_completed_focus = GRE_bedrock_of_balkan_financial_stability
            has_completed_focus = GRE_economic_fluidity_plans
        }
        
        visible = {
            has_completed_focus = GRE_tariff
            if = {
                limit = {
                    FROM = { is_major = no }
                }
                check_variable = { FROM.favor@GRE > 49 }
            }
            FROM = {
                OR = {
                    has_idea = GRtar_trade_1
                    has_idea = GRtar_trade_2 
                    has_idea = GRtar_trade_3
                }
            }
            NOT = { has_country_flag = toggle_tariff }
        }

        cost = 0

		fire_only_once = no

		days_remove = 0

		complete_effect = {
            FROM = { 
                if = {
                    limit = {
                        has_idea = GRtar_trade_3
                    }
                    swap_ideas = {
                        remove_idea = GRtar_trade_3
                        add_idea = GRtar_trade_2
                    }
                    set_variable = { GRE.tariff_level@FROM = 2 }
                }
                else_if = {
                    limit = {
                        has_idea = GRtar_trade_2
                    }
                    swap_ideas = {
                        remove_idea = GRtar_trade_2
                        add_idea = GRtar_trade_1
                    }
                    set_variable = { GRE.tariff_level@FROM = 1 }
                }
                else = {
                    remove_ideas = GRtar_trade_1
                    set_variable = { GRE.tariff_level@FROM = 0 }
                }
            }
		}    
    }

    GRE_expand_collapse_mining_rights_decisions = {
        icon = decision_generic_decision
    
        allowed = { tag=GRE }
        
        fire_only_once = no

        available = { has_completed_focus=GRE_public_works }
        visible = { check_variable={ var=amount_of_projects value=4 compare=greater_than_or_equals }}

        custom_cost_trigger = {
            set_temp_variable={ base=100 }
            add_to_temp_variable={ base=var:kathestos_dynamic_ppcost }
            has_political_power>base
        }
        custom_cost_text = met_dyn_cost
        complete_effect = { 
            hidden_effect={
                set_temp_variable={ base=100 }
                add_to_temp_variable={ base=var:kathestos_dynamic_ppcost }
                multiply_temp_variable={ base=-1 }
                add_political_power=base
            }
            add_to_variable={ kathestos_dynamic_ppcost=25 }
        }
        remove_effect = { add_to_variable={ kathestos_dynamic_ppcost=-25 }}

		remove_effect = {
			add_stability = 0.01
            add_to_variable = { amount_of_projects=1 tooltip=projects_increased_tt }
            ###[ METAXAS PLAN MECHANIC ]###
            custom_effect_tooltip = met_dyn_up_tt
            add_to_variable={ GRE_var_aa=0.03 tooltip=met_infr_tt }
            add_to_variable={ repair_speed_factor=0.02 tooltip=met_rep_tt }  
            add_to_variable={ GRE_var_civ=0.03 tooltip=met_civ_tt }
            add_to_variable={ GRE_var_mil=0.03 tooltip=met_mil_tt }  
            ###BUILDINGS###
            custom_effect_tooltip = works_equals_infr_tt
            set_country_flag = funded_flood_works
            if = {
                limit = { has_country_flag=funded_flood_works has_country_flag=funded_dry_works }
                every_state = {
                    limit={ is_controlled_by=GRE}
                    add_building_construction = { type=infrastructure level=1 instant_build=yes }
                }
                clr_country_flag = funded_flood_works
                clr_country_flag = funded_dry_works
            }
            ###################################
            if = {
                limit = { OR={ has_active_mission=GRE_repub_upr has_active_mission=GRE_comm_upr has_active_mission=workers_entering_factories has_active_mission=invigorating_hellenic_spirit }}
                
                custom_effect_tooltip = mis_impacts_header
            }
            if = {
                limit = { has_active_mission = GRE_repub_upr }

                set_temp_variable={ tmpMISS=1 }
                set_temp_variable={ tmpSIGN=0 }
                set_temp_variable={ tmpARD=5 }
                set_temp_variable={ tmpDIS=5 }
                custom_effect_tooltip = mis_impact
                hidden_effect={ add_days_mission_timeout={ mission=GRE_repub_upr days=tmpARD }}
            }
            if = {
                limit = { has_active_mission = GRE_comm_upr }

                set_temp_variable={ tmpMISS=0 }
                set_temp_variable={ tmpSIGN=0 }
                set_temp_variable={ tmpARD=5 }
                set_temp_variable={ tmpDIS=5 }
                custom_effect_tooltip = mis_impact
                hidden_effect={ add_days_mission_timeout={ mission=GRE_comm_upr days=tmpARD }}
            }
            if = {
                limit = { has_active_mission=workers_entering_factories }

                set_temp_variable={ tmpMISS=2 }
                set_temp_variable={ tmpSIGN=0 }
                set_temp_variable={ tmpARD=-30 }
                set_temp_variable={ tmpDIS=30 }
                custom_effect_tooltip = mis_impact
                hidden_effect={ add_days_mission_timeout={ mission=workers_entering_factories days=tmpARD }}
            }
            if = {
                limit = { has_active_mission=invigorating_hellenic_spirit }

                set_temp_variable={ tmpMISS=3 }
                set_temp_variable={ tmpSIGN=0 }
                set_temp_variable={ tmpARD=-45 }
                set_temp_variable={ tmpDIS=45 }
                custom_effect_tooltip = mis_impact
                hidden_effect={ add_days_mission_timeout={ mission=invigorating_hellenic_spirit days=tmpARD }}
            }
            ###FACTION MECHANICS###
            set_temp_dem_insignificant_positive = yes
            set_temp_com_insignificant_positive = yes
            set_temp_fas_insignificant_positive = yes
            set_temp_mon_insignificant_positive = yes
		}

    fix_inaccessible_regions = {
		icon = industry

		allowed = { tag=GRE }
        
		fire_only_once = yes
        days_remove = 180

        custom_cost_trigger = {
            set_temp_variable={ base=125 }
            add_to_temp_variable={ base=var:kathestos_dynamic_ppcost }
            has_political_power>base
        }
        custom_cost_text = met_dyn_cost
        complete_effect = { 
            hidden_effect={
                set_temp_variable={ base=125 }
                add_to_temp_variable={ base=var:kathestos_dynamic_ppcost }
                multiply_temp_variable={ base=-1 }
                add_political_power=base
            }
            add_to_variable={ kathestos_dynamic_ppcost=25 }
        }
        remove_effect = { add_to_variable={ kathestos_dynamic_ppcost=-25 }}

		available = {
            has_idea = GRE_aristeidis_dimitratos_political_advisor 
            set_temp_variable = { tmpPR=14 }
            custom_trigger_tooltip = {
                tooltip=more_than_tmpPR_projects
                check_variable = { var=amount_of_projects value=tmpPR compare=greater_than_or_equals }
            }
		}

		visible = { check_variable={ var=amount_of_projects value=4 compare=greater_than_or_equals }}

		cancel_if_not_visible = no


		remove_effect = {
            add_to_variable = { amount_of_projects=1 tooltip=projects_increased_tt }  
            every_controlled_state = {
                if = {
                    limit={ has_dynamic_modifier={ modifier=GRE_inaccessible_region }}
                    remove_dynamic_modifier={ modifier=GRE_inaccessible_region }
                }
            }
            #######################
            if = {
                limit = { OR={ has_active_mission=workers_entering_factories has_active_mission=invigorating_hellenic_spirit }}
                
                custom_effect_tooltip = mis_impacts_header
            }

            #######################
            if = {
