                limit = { OR={ has_active_mission=GRE_repub_upr has_active_mission=GRE_comm_upr has_active_mission=workers_entering_factories has_active_mission=invigorating_hellenic_spirit }}
                
                custom_effect_tooltip = mis_impacts_header
            }
            if = {
                limit = { has_active_mission = GRE_repub_upr }

                set_temp_variable={ tmpMISS=1 }
                set_temp_variable={ tmpSIGN=0 }
                set_temp_variable={ tmpARD=5 }
                set_temp_variable={ tmpDIS=5 }
                custom_effect_tooltip = mis_impact
                hidden_effect={
                    add_days_mission_timeout = { mission = GRE_repub_upr days = tmpARD }
                }
            }
            if = {
                limit = { has_active_mission = GRE_comm_upr }

                set_temp_variable={ tmpMISS=0 }
                set_temp_variable={ tmpSIGN=0 }
                set_temp_variable={ tmpARD=30 }
                set_temp_variable={ tmpDIS=30 }
                custom_effect_tooltip = mis_impact
                hidden_effect={
                    add_days_mission_timeout = { mission = GRE_comm_upr days = tmpARD }
                }
            }
            if = {
                limit = { has_active_mission=workers_entering_factories }

                set_temp_variable={ tmpMISS=2 }
                set_temp_variable={ tmpSIGN=1 }
                set_temp_variable={ tmpARD=12 }
                set_temp_variable={ tmpDIS=12 }
                custom_effect_tooltip = mis_impact
                hidden_effect={ add_days_mission_timeout={ mission=workers_entering_factories days=tmpARD }}
            }
            if = {
                limit = { has_active_mission=invigorating_hellenic_spirit }

                set_temp_variable={ tmpMISS=3 }
                set_temp_variable={ tmpSIGN=1 }
                set_temp_variable={ tmpARD=12 }
                set_temp_variable={ tmpDIS=12 }
                custom_effect_tooltip = mis_impact
                hidden_effect={ add_days_mission_timeout={ mission=invigorating_hellenic_spirit days=tmpARD }}
            }
            #######################
            custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_change_shrt_title
            if = {
                limit={ set_temp_variable={ tmpF=1 } is_faction_tmpF_below_tmpZ=yes }
                set_temp_variable = { tmp_dem_effect_decrease = 0.02 }
                set_temp_variable = { tmp_dem_effect = fct_dem_effect_multiplier }
                subtract_from_temp_variable = { tmp_dem_effect = tmp_dem_effect_decrease }
                set_variable = { fct_dem_effect_multiplier = tmp_dem_effect }
                custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_change_shrt_down_dem
            }
            if = {
                limit={ set_temp_variable={ tmpF=2 } is_faction_tmpF_below_tmpZ=yes }
                set_temp_variable = { tmp_com_effect_decrease = 0.04 }
                set_temp_variable = { tmp_com_effect = fct_com_effect_multiplier }
                subtract_from_temp_variable = { tmp_com_effect = tmp_com_effect_decrease }
                set_variable = { fct_com_effect_multiplier = tmp_com_effect }
                custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_change_shrt_down_com
            }
            if = {
                limit={ set_temp_variable={ tmpF=3 } is_faction_tmpF_below_tmpZ=yes }
                set_temp_variable = { tmp_fas_effect_decrease = 0.06 }
                set_temp_variable = { tmp_fas_effect = fct_fas_effect_multiplier }
                subtract_from_temp_variable = { tmp_fas_effect = tmp_fas_effect_decrease }
                set_variable = { fct_fas_effect_multiplier = tmp_fas_effect }
                custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_change_shrt_down_fas
            }
            if = {
                limit={ set_temp_variable={ tmpF=0 } is_faction_tmpF_below_tmpZ=yes }
                set_temp_variable = { tmp_mon_effect_decrease = 0.03 }
                set_temp_variable = { tmp_mon_effect = fct_mon_effect_multiplier }
                subtract_from_temp_variable = { tmp_mon_effect = tmp_mon_effect_decrease }
                set_variable = { fct_mon_effect_multiplier = tmp_mon_effect }
                custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_change_shrt_down_mon
            }
            #######################
            ###FACTION MECHANICS###
            set_temp_variable={ tmpZ=80 }
            set_temp_variable={ tmpF=1 }
            if = { limit={ is_faction_tmpF_at_least_tmpZ=yes } set_temp_dem_favourable=yes }
            else_if = { limit={ is_faction_tmpF_hostile=no } set_temp_dem_beneficial=yes }
            else ={ set_temp_dem_detrimental=yes }
            set_temp_variable={ tmpF=2 }
            if = { limit={ is_faction_tmpF_at_least_tmpZ=yes } set_temp_com_extremely_favourable=yes }
            else_if = { limit={ is_faction_tmpF_hostile=no } set_temp_com_favourable=yes }
            else ={ set_temp_com_adverse=yes }
            set_temp_variable={ tmpF=3 }
            if = { limit={ is_faction_tmpF_at_least_tmpZ=yes } set_temp_fas_immense=yes }
            else_if = { limit={ is_faction_tmpF_hostile=no } set_temp_fas_extremely_favourable=yes }
            else ={ set_temp_fas_adverse=yes }
            set_temp_variable={ tmpF=0 }
            if = { limit={ is_faction_tmpF_at_least_tmpZ=yes } set_temp_mon_extremely_favourable=yes }
            else_if = { limit={ is_faction_tmpF_hostile=no } set_temp_mon_favourable=yes }
            else ={ set_temp_mon_detrimental=yes }
            custom_effect_tooltip = decision_dynamic_affect_three_ways_tmpZ
        }
    }

            add_dynamic_modifier={ modifier=GRE_army_reform_hellenic_staff }
            add_dynamic_modifier={ modifier=GRE_army_reform_hellenic_army }  
            if = {
                limit = {
                    check_variable = { var = GRE_army_reform_cnt value = 15 compare = less_than_or_equals }
                    has_idea = GRE_army_status_0
                }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = GRE_army_status_0
					add_idea = GRE_army_status_1
				}
                set_variable = { GRE_ges = 1 }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    check_variable = { var = GRE_army_reform_cnt value = 15 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
                    has_idea = GRE_army_status_0
                }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = GRE_army_status_0
					add_idea = GRE_army_status_2
				}
                set_variable = { GRE_ges = 2 }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    has_idea = GRE_army_status_1
                }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = GRE_army_status_1
					add_idea = GRE_army_status_2
				}
                set_variable = { GRE_ges = 2 }   
            }
        }

                check_variable = { GRE_debt_to_the_ifc_italy_var = 0 compare = less_than_or_equals }
            }
		}

		visible = {
            has_completed_focus = GRE_the_italian_question
            NOT = { has_war_with = ITA }
            NOT = { has_country_flag = GRE_italians_responded }
            ITA = { has_government = fascism }
            GER = { has_government = fascism }
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}

		fire_only_once = no

		days_remove = 90

        cost = 75
        fixed_random_seed = no
        
        remove_effect = {               ### THE FOLLOWING CALCULATES THE FAVOR OF BOTH ITALY AND THE GERMANS (weighted 80% for italians, 20% for germans) and slowly drags the readiness variable towards 100, where italians will accept rapproachment###
            if = {
                limit = {
                    check_variable = { GRE_italian_readiness = 100 compare = less_than_or_equals }
                }
                random_list = {
                    85 = {
                        custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_italian_rapproachment_85_tt
                        set_temp_variable = { x = ITA.favor@GRE }
                        set_temp_variable = { y = GER.favor@GRE }
                        clamp_temp_variable = {
                            var = x
                            min = 0
                            max = 100                       
                        }
                        clamp_temp_variable = {
                            var = y
                            min = 0
                            max = 100                       
                        }                        
                        multiply_temp_variable = { x = 0.8 }
                        multiply_temp_variable = { y = 0.2 } 
                        add_to_temp_variable = { x = y }
                        multiply_temp_variable = { x = 0.5 } 
                        add_to_variable = { GRE_italian_readiness = x }
                    }
                    10 = {
                        custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_italian_rapproachment_10_tt
                        subtract_from_variable = { GRE_italian_readiness = 5 }
                    }
                    5 = {
                        custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_italian_rapproachment_5_tt
                        set_country_flag = GRE_italians_responded
                        hidden_effect = {
                            country_event = { id = hellas.323 days = 0 }  
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            else = {
                set_country_flag = GRE_italians_responded
                country_event = { id = hellas.323 days = 0 }
            }
        }
    }

    ### Balkan Pact Investments ###

    greek_subsidized_factories = {
        icon = industry
        allowed = { tag = GRE }
        on_map_mode = map_and_decisions_view
        highlight_states = { highlight_states_trigger = { state = FROM.capital } }
        
        targets = {	TUR YUG ROM BUL ALB }

		target_trigger = {
            country_exists = FROM
			FROM = { has_country_flag = balkan_pact_reinforced }
            NOT = { has_global_flag = GRE_grecoitalian_start }
            NOT = { has_axis_occupation = yes }
		}

        available = {
            GRE = { num_of_civilian_factories_available_for_projects > 10 }
            FROM = {
                has_political_power > 50 
                custom_trigger_tooltip = {
                    tooltip = no_gsfc_tt
                    NOT = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_greek_subsidized_factories_cost } }
                }
            }
        }

        fire_only_once = no
        days_remove = 60

        modifier = { civilian_factory_use = 10 }

        complete_effect = {
            add_political_power = 200                           ### We get payed upfront, cause we ain't dummies
            ####################################                ### Phase 1, they pay base 50 upfront
            set_variable = { FROM.gre_gsfc = -0.75 }                ### Phase 2, they pay base 45 daily (45/60=0.75)
            set_variable = { FROM.gre_ifd  = 5 }                 ## They also contribute with 5 civs
            FROM = {
                add_political_power = -50
                add_dynamic_modifier = {
                    modifier = GRE_greek_subsidized_factories_cost
                    days = 270
                }
                custom_effect_tooltip = gsfc_tt
            }
        }

        remove_effect = {
            set_variable = { FROM.gre_gsfc = -0.5 }         ### They pay the rest 105 over 210 days.
            set_variable = { FROM.gre_ifd = 0 }              ## Their civ contribution is over
            FROM = {
                set_temp_variable={ tmpAW=0.50 } 
                add_to_variable = { balkan_pact_desirability=tmpAW } 
                refresh_balkan_pact_desirability_gui_THIS=yes
                custom_effect_tooltip = alliance_weight_increased_tmpAW_tt
                random_owned_controlled_state = {
                    add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
                    add_building_construction = { type = industrial_complex level = 1 instant_build = yes }
                    add_building_construction = { type = arms_factory level = 1 instant_build = yes }
                }
                clear_variable = gre_ifd
            }
            set_temp_variable = { findX = FROM.id }
            set_temp_variable = { findY = 10 }
            custom_effect_tooltip = "      "
            custom_effect_tooltip = favor_boost_with_findX_by_findY
            add_to_variable = { GRE.civs_given@FROM = 1 }
            add_to_variable = { GRE.mils_given@FROM = 1 }
        }
    }

	GRE_comm_upr = {

        on_map_mode = map_and_decisions_view
        highlight_states = {
 			highlight_state_targets = { state = 185 } 
 			#highlight_color_before_active = 3

		}

		available = {
            set_temp_variable = { tmpZ = 40 }
            OR = {
                com_is_at_least_tmpZ = yes
                custom_trigger_tooltip = {
                    tooltip = comm_uppr_dealt_other_ways_tt
                    has_country_flag = communist_uprising_utterly_crushed
                }
            }
		}

		days_mission_timeout = 95
        fire_only_once = yes
		activation = { has_country_flag = GRE_comm_upr_1 }
        visible = { has_country_flag = GRE_comm_upr_1 }
		cancel_if_not_visible = no
		is_good = no

		complete_effect = {
            clr_country_flag = GRE_comm_upr_1
            add_stability = 0.02
            add_to_variable = { fct_com = 2.5 }
            faction_gui_call = yes
		}

		timeout_effect = {
            set_temp_variable = { x = party_popularity@communism }
            ###[Take the highest between Representation and Overall Military Grip]###
            set_temp_variable = { y = GRE.com_asgn_w }
            multiply_temp_variable = { y = 0.04 }
            set_temp_variable = { tmpF = 2 }
            calculate_mg_percentage = yes
            if = { limit = { check_variable = { y < mg } } set_temp_variable = { y = mg } }
            ###[Multiply and Clamp]###
            multiply_temp_variable = { x = y }
            clamp_temp_variable = {
                var = x
                min = 0.02
                max = 0.85
            }
            ###[Start Civil War]###
            start_civil_war = {
                ruling_party = ROOT
                ideology = communism
                size = x
                capital = 47
                states = { 185 911 912 }
                keep_unit_leaders_trigger = { has_trait = trait_GRE_stauch_communist_persona }
                keep_political_leader = yes
            }
            set_country_flag = com_civilwar_started
		}
	}

            original_tag = GRE

                limit = {

            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    GRE = { is_ai = yes }
                }
                GRE = { change_tag_from = ROOT }
            }
        }
    
    }

    #############################################[ PLAYER-BASED DECISIONS ]#############################################
    #############################################[ ON MAP DECISIONS ]#############################################
    GRE_expand_collapse_black_market_icons = {
        icon = decision_generic_decision
    
        allowed = { tag=GRE }
        
        fire_only_once = no
        days_remove = 0
        days_re_enable = 0
        priority = 10
        
        visible = { has_axis_occupation=yes }
        
        complete_effect = {
            hidden_effect = {
                if = {
                    limit = {
                        NOT = { has_country_flag = hide_black_market_icons }
                    }
                    set_country_flag = hide_black_market_icons
                }
                else = {
                    clr_country_flag = hide_black_market_icons 
                }
            }
        }
    }
    add_black_0 = {
		icon = GFX_icon_black_0
        state_target = yes
        target_array = global.greek_occupied_states_all
		available = {
            original_tag = GRE
            if = { limit = { has_country_flag = black_market_option_invest } 
                if = { limit = { FROM = { state = 47 } } has_political_power > 25 }
                else_if = { limit = { FROM = { OR = { state = 913 state = 731 state = 186 state = 910} } } has_political_power > 15 }
                else = { has_political_power > 10 }
            }
		}
		on_map_mode = map_only
		fire_only_once = no
		days_remove = 0

		visible = {
            FROM = { 
                NOT = {
                    has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = black_market_obscure }
                    has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = black_market_cemented }
                    has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = black_market_ubshakeable }
                    has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = black_market_obscure_controlled }
                    has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = black_market_cemented_controlled }
                    has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = black_market_ubshakeable_controlled }
                }
            }
            NOT = { has_country_flag = hide_black_market_icons }
            has_country_flag = black_market_option_invest
		}
		remove_effect = {
            ###[State Weight]###
            if = {
                limit = { has_country_flag = black_market_option_invest } 
                FROM = { HS_BM_add_negative_level = yes }
                if = { limit = { FROM = { state = 47 } } add_political_power = -25 }
                else_if = { limit = { FROM = { OR = { state = 913 state = 731 state = 186 state = 910} } } add_political_power = -15 }
                else = { add_political_power = -10 }
            }
		}
	} 
    
    add_black_1 = {
		icon = GFX_icon_black_1_negative
        state_target = yes
        target_array = global.greek_occupied_states_all
		available = {
            original_tag = GRE
            if = { limit = { has_country_flag = black_market_option_crackdown } 
                if = { limit = { FROM = { state = 47 } } has_political_power > 100 }
                else_if = { limit = { FROM = { OR = { state = 913 state = 731 state = 186 state = 910} } } has_political_power > 75 }
                else = { has_political_power > 50 }
            }
            else_if = { limit = { has_country_flag = black_market_option_invest } 
                if = { limit = { FROM = { state = 47 } } has_political_power > 25 }
                else_if = { limit = { FROM = { OR = { state = 913 state = 731 state = 186 state = 910} } } has_political_power > 15 }
                else = { has_political_power > 10 }
            }
		}
		on_map_mode = map_only

		days_remove = 0

                has_country_flag = black_market_option_invest

		}
		remove_effect = {

                limit = { has_country_flag = black_market_option_crackdown } 
                FROM = { HS_BM_reduce_level = yes }
                if = { limit = { FROM = { state = 47 } } add_political_power = -100 }
                else_if = { limit = { FROM = { OR = { state = 913 state = 731 state = 186 state = 910} } } add_political_power = -75 }
                else = { add_political_power = -50 }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = { has_country_flag = black_market_option_invest } 
                FROM = { HS_BM_add_negative_level = yes }
                if = { limit = { FROM = { state = 47 } } add_political_power = -25 }
                else_if = { limit = { FROM = { OR = { state = 913 state = 731 state = 186 state = 910} } } add_political_power = -15 }

            else_if = { limit = { FROM = { OR = { state = 913 state = 731 state = 186 state = 910} } } has_political_power > 175 }
            else = { has_political_power > 150 }
		}
		on_map_mode = map_only
		fire_only_once = no
		days_remove = 0

		visible = {
            FROM = { 
                FROM = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = black_market_obscure_controlled } }
            }
            NOT = { has_country_flag = hide_black_market_icons }
            has_country_flag = black_market_option_invest
		}
		remove_effect = {
            FROM = { HS_BM_add_positive_level = yes }
            if = { limit = { FROM = { state = 47 } } add_political_power = -200 }
            else_if = { limit = { FROM = { OR = { state = 913 state = 731 state = 186 state = 910} } } add_political_power = -175 }
            else = { add_political_power = -150 }
		}
	}

    GRE_expand_collapse_add_greeks_icons = {
        icon = decision_generic_decision
    
        allowed = { tag=GRE }
        
        fire_only_once = no
        days_remove = 0
        days_re_enable = 0
        priority = 10
        
        visible = { has_axis_occupation=yes }
        
        complete_effect = {
            hidden_effect = {
                if = {
                    limit = {
                        NOT = { has_country_flag = hide_unyielding_greeks_icons }
                    }
                    set_country_flag = hide_unyielding_greeks_icons
                }
                else = {
                    clr_country_flag = hide_unyielding_greeks_icons 
                }
            }
        }
    }
